### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value.

### SPARQL:iconductorX1
###
CONDITIONAL_GENE_X1 = "APOC1"
POST_JUVENILE_X1 = "post-juvenile"
ANATOMICAL_ENTITY_X1 = "anatomical entity"
ANATOMICAL_ENTITY_SCIENTIFIC_NAME_X1 = "anatomical entity scientific name"
GENE_EXPRESSION_X1 = "gene expression"
GENE_EXPRESSION_HAS_FALSE_DISCOVERY_RATE_P_VALUE_X1 = "gene expression has false discovery rate p-value"

PREFIX condition:<http://purl.org/dc/terms/condition>
PREFIX gene:<http://purl.org/dc/terms/gene>
PREFIX expression:<http://purl.org/dc/terms/expression>
PREFIX x1:<http://purl.org/x1/generation/condition/individual/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x4 ?x2 ?x0 ?x1_hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x5 ?x4Name ?x2Name WHERE { 
	?x0 a condition:Condition .
	?x1 a expression:Expression .
	?x1 condition:hasExpressionCondition ?x2 .
	?x1 condition:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 condition:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 gene:GENERATES ?x4 .
	?x4 a efo:EFO_0005152 .
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1 condition:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x2 .
	?x2 rdfs:label ?x2Name .
	?x1 condition:hasAnatomicalEntityCondition ?x5 .
	?x5 a condition:AnatomicalEntityCondition.
	?x5 condition:hasAnatomicalEntityType ?x6 .
	?x6 a condition:AnatomicalEntityType.
	?x1 condition:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x1_hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value .
	?x1_hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value a condition:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1_hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value condition:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x7 .
	?x7 rdfs:label ?x7_x1hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_valueAnatomicalEntity .
	?x7 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName> ?x7_x1hasexpression_hasfalsediscoveryratep_valueAnatomicalEntityScientificName .
	FILTER(             ?x2 != condition:CellType .
	FILTER(             ?x2 != condition:Strain .
	FILTER(             ?x2 != condition:Individual .
	FILTER(             ?x4 != efo:EFO_0005151 .
	FILTER(             ?x4 != "human" .
	FILTER(             ?x2 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/scientificName> ?x2_x2Name .
	FILTER(             ?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	FILTER(             ?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> fp:url .
	FILTER(             ?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/identifier> ?x0_x0 .

### EXPLANATION:
<pre>
http://www.ebi.ac.uk/efo/EFO_0000393?xuniprot=P0D0R1&xcondition=post-juvenile&xanatomicalentity=human provides the gene identifier.
http://purl.org/dc/terms/xuniprot?xuniprot=P0D0R1 provides the uniprot identifier.
http://purl.org/dc/terms/xcondition?xcondition=post-juvenile provides the condition.
http://purl.org/dc/terms/xanatomicalentity?xanatomicalentity=human provides the anatomical entity.
</pre>

### SPARQL:

PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>

PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>

	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x9 .
	?x9 obo:RO_0002162  ?x10 .
	?x10 a up:Taxon .
	?x10 up:commonName "human" .
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x10_scientificname.
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x10_commonname.
	?x8 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x8_label.
	?x8 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x8_description.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != ?x6                 )
}

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:iconductorX
###
CONDITIONAL_FORMAT:conditionals_format
SELECT DISTINCT ?x1condition ?x4_label ?x1 ?x3 ?x4 ?x1_seealso ?x0 ?x0_label WHERE { 
	?x0 a efo:Gene .
	?x1 a efo:Expression .
	?x1 efo:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 efo:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 efo:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a efo:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition efo:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a efo:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1condition efo:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label "juvenile" .
	?x1condition efo:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition efo:hasStrain ?x7 .
	?x7 a efo:Strain.
	?x7 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	FILTER(     ?x4 !=  ?x1condition     )
}
ORDER BY ?x4 ?x4_label
### ANSWER:
?x1condition ?x4 ?x4_label ?x1 ?x0 ?x0_label ?x0_seealso
### EXPLANATION:

	?x1 rdfs:label ?human .
	}

	?x1 rdfs:label ?x0_label .

	}

	?x4 rdfs:label ?x2Name .

	}

	}

### INSTRUCTION

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities where the human gene APOC1 is expressed in the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain, sex, and cell type? Provide also the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
PREFIX up-taxon:<http://purl.uniprot.org/taxonomy/>
PREFIX ensembl: <http://rdf.ebi.ac.uk/resource/ensembl/>
PREFIX lscr: <http://purl.org/lscr#>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x1condition ?x4_label ?x4_description ?x4 ?x4Name ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x1 ?x3 ?x6 ?x6_label ?x0_description ?x0 ?x0_seealso ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 lscr:xrefEnsemblGene ensembl:ENSG00000130208 .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.

	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage obo:UBERON_0000113 .
	?x1condition genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition genex:hasStrain ?x6 .
	?x6 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?x6 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x6 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x6_label.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
	FILTER(               ?x4 !=  obo:GO_0005575               )
}
ORDER BY ?x4 ?x4Name

### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x1 ?x3 ?x8_description ?x1condition ?x4_description ?x8 ?x10_scientificname ?x9 ?x4_label ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x8_label ?x10 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x0 ?x0_label ?x10_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x9 .
	?x9 obo:RO_0002162  ?x10 .
	?x10 a up:Taxon .
	?x10 up:commonName "human" .
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x10_scientificname.
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x10_commonname.
	?x8 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x8_label.
	?x8 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x8_description.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x0_label.
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != ?x6                 )
}

	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the developmental stage label and the developmental stage description and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x8_description ?x1 ?x3 ?x1condition ?x4_description ?x8 ?x10_scientificname ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x9 ?x4_label ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x0_seealso ?x8_label ?x10 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x0 ?x10_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdf:type efo:EFO_0000399 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x9 .
	?x9 obo:RO_0002162  ?x10 .
	?x10 a up:Taxon .
	?x10 up:commonName "human" .
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x10_scientificname.
	?x10 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x10_commonname.
	?x8 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x8_label.
	?x8 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x8_description.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	FILTER(                 ?x4 !=  obo:GO_0005575                 )
	FILTER(                 ?x4 != ?x6                 )
}
ORDER BY ?x4 ?x4Name ?x0 ?x1 ?x1condition ?x4_label ?x8 ?x0_seealso ?x4_description ?x8_scientificname ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x4 ?x4Name

<http://www.humanconnectome.org/cgi-bin/sparql?query=SELECT DISTINCT %0A%09%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E%5E

101:
### INSTRUCTION
Please convert the following context into an SPARQL query.

### CONTEXT:
What are the anatomical entities including cell types, if any, where the human gene APOC1 is expressed at the post-juvenile stage along with its expression score independently of the strain and sex? Provide also the taxon scientific name and the taxon common name and the strain label and the anatomical entity label and the anatomical entity description and the gene expression has expression level score and the gene expression has false discovery rate p-value and the gene see also and the gene description and the gene label.

### SPARQL:
PREFIX orth: <http://purl.org/net/orth#>
PREFIX genex: <http://purl.org/genex#>
PREFIX obo: <http://purl.obolibrary.org/obo/>
PREFIX up: <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/>
SELECT DISTINCT ?x6 ?x1 ?x3 ?x1condition ?x4_description ?x11_scientificname ?x9_label ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value ?x10 ?x4_label ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x8 ?x0_label ?x11 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x0_description ?x9 ?x0 ?x0_seealso ?x11_commonname WHERE { 
	?x0 a orth:Gene .
	?x1 a genex:Expression .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionCondition ?x1condition .
	?x1 genex:hasExpressionLevel ?x3 .
	?x1 genex:hasSequenceUnit ?x0 .
	?x0 rdfs:label "APOC1" .
	?x1condition a genex:ExpressionCondition.
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x4 .
	?x4 a genex:AnatomicalEntity.
	?x4 rdfs:label ?x4Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasAnatomicalEntity ?x6 .
	?x6 rdfs:label ?x6Name .
	?x1condition genex:hasDevelopmentalStage ?x8 .
	?x8 rdfs:label "post-juvenile" .
	?x1condition genex:hasSex "any".
	?x1condition genex:hasStrain ?x9 .
	?x9 a efo:EFO_0005135.
	?x9 rdfs:label "wild-type" .
	?x0 orth:organism ?x10 .
	?x10 obo:RO_0002162  ?x11 .
	?x11 a up:Taxon .
	?x11 up:commonName "human" .
	?x11 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/scientificName> ?x11_scientificname.
	?x11 <http://purl.uniprot.org/core/commonName> ?x11_commonname.
	?x9 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x9_label.
	?x4 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x4_label.
	?x4 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x4_description.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasExpressionLevel> ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore.
	?x1 <http://purl.org/genex#hasFDRpvalue> ?x1_hasfalsediscoveryratep_value.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#seeAlso> ?x0_seealso.
	?x0 <http://purl.org/dc/terms/description> ?x0_description.
	?x0 <http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label> ?x0_label.
	FILTER(                     ?x4 != obo:GO_0005575                     )
	FILTER(                     ?x4 != ?x6                     )
}

### OUTPUT:
###
### http://www.w3.org/2000/01/rdf-schema#label ?x0_label ?x4_label ?x11_scientificname ?x0_description ?x9_label ?x1_hasexpressionlevelscore ?x0 ?x0_seealso ?x11 ?x4 ?x4Name ?x6Name ?x1 <http://purl

### CONTEXT:
